<div id="review_1446359769" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1446359769" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1446359769?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Aj the Ravenous Reader by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=not-for-me">not-for-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=definitely-not-young-adult">definitely-not-young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1446359769" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3204108352549014408"><br/>The story started out nicely and the plot, though predictable was laid out satisfactorily following the generic NA formula- two nice people with broken, painful past somehow finding each other in a small town. The mild twist is that Archer couldn’t talk, “a beautiful, silent man”. (Bree made sure I knew that because she mentioned it only a couple hundred times.^^) It’s told by the alternating voices of Bree and Archer but mostly by Bree. Her narrative, though a bit monotonous and unnecessarily d</span>
  <span id="freeText3204108352549014408" style="display:none"><br />The story started out nicely and the plot, though predictable was laid out satisfactorily following the generic NA formula- two nice people with broken, painful past somehow finding each other in a small town. The mild twist is that Archer couldn’t talk, “a beautiful, silent man”. (Bree made sure I knew that because she mentioned it only a couple hundred times.^^) It’s told by the alternating voices of Bree and Archer but mostly by Bree. Her narrative, though a bit monotonous and unnecessarily detailed (“I brushed my teeth...I used the curling iron to curl my hair”), was forgivable because anyway it’s just the beginning. The introduction even reminded me of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2345.Nicholas_Sparks" title="Nicholas Sparks" rel="nofollow noopener">Nicholas Sparks</a> novels- sweet and comfy at start, just prepare oneself for the tragic ending.<br /><br />But then Bree cut Archer’s shaggy hair and then, holy burnin’ smokes! The story drastically turned into a hundred percent erotica or perhaps my copy was just defective because I’m pretty sure somebody printed the wrong half of the book and printed the pages of a manual teaching how to enhance somebody’s sexual life. <b>*insert peace sign here.*</b><br /><br />It’s not that I’m against that, it’s just that I honestly didn’t expect this to be that blatant. I was eager for that “lyrical” narrative about true love and moving on and stuff like those but unfortunately, I found nothing poetic about the severely strong sexual language that would describe intimate moments unabashedly and would take up fifty percent of the entire book’s pages. Personally, I’d like that wonderful aspect of life to leave me a little room for imagination the way <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a> for example, would do it.^^<br /><br />Two things good about the book though: The happy ending (Nicholas Sparks lost this round, ha!) and giving me plenty of chances to exercise my facial muscles from too much cringing.^^<br /><br />Gah! I’m really sorry. I don’t mean to offend anyone, especially not my friends who loved this book. This is just clearly not for me. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli" rel="nofollow noopener">Pearl</a>, I’m going to have to read another book for your birthday. <br /><br />Maybe, I just really read this the wrong way or maybe I read the wrong book so please do not pay too much attention on this review and do read my wonderful friends' reviews. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1097017771?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Pearl's</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/968541011?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Beatrice's</a>.<br /><br />*Bracing myself for the rotten tomatoes I'm sure will come my way*<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3204108352549014408" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1806441587?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" href="/user/show/19719801-xxtainaxx-curvy-and-nerdy">XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1806441587" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12301426128673099419">Audiobook review. While I run away from my lovely super fan friends, I will say that I honestly struggled with the narration, where errors in the prose seemed to be more noticeable. Hearing them is certainly different from reading them. I am glad that I stuck to the story, however, because I would've missed out on a pretty great tale. <br/><br/>The underlying theme of this book was very refreshing. The characters are unique and flawed. They make their own place in your heart. Bree found a treasure hidden </span>
  <span id="freeText12301426128673099419" style="display:none">Audiobook review. While I run away from my lovely super fan friends, I will say that I honestly struggled with the narration, where errors in the prose seemed to be more noticeable. Hearing them is certainly different from reading them. I am glad that I stuck to the story, however, because I would've missed out on a pretty great tale. <br /><br />The underlying theme of this book was very refreshing. The characters are unique and flawed. They make their own place in your heart. Bree found a treasure hidden away when she and Archer crossed paths. It was amazing to read/hear as she peeled away his layers. He was good for her too. He created the space she needed to heal. I was happy that she found her home. The innocence and eagerness that Archer exuded translated well in different aspects of the story, from his first movie to his first kiss and more. The plot was interesting, properly paced, and executed well. My emotions were certainly engaged by the story and in more ways than the romance aspect. I don't think I remember hating a character more than Travis. One part had me crying in anger and emotion! This is a solid story with an enlivening composition.<br /><br />Safety: No rape. There is abuse. H does have a sensual interaction with OW but there's more to this than meets the eye. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12301426128673099419" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Their love for one another was just so sweet. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/6F6B01EA-AD78-411F-96D1-CC3AC036AA80_zpsgdm7yss0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478745603i/21107604._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 90C31068-21BA-4264-8753-66D0223FE67F_zpssigywyhv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Bree moved to the small town to hopefully escape her nightmares of the tragedy that she lived through. She was so sweet and so thankful to make new friends. The moment she saw Archer, she was intrigued by him. She wanted to get to know him but no matter what she did, she could not get a reaction out of him. Finally she wore him down and he started opening up to her. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/A02B9A43-266D-4DCE-BE31-432384A06481_zps0ngmaqry.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478745603i/21107605.jpg" alt=" photo A02B9A43-266D-4DCE-BE31-432384A06481_zps0ngmaqry.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They both had things to work through and it was hard but they worked through it together. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/FE75720B-936F-472C-8F0F-095D57EB75B8_zpsaxtwvrhx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478745603i/21107606.jpg" alt=" photo FE75720B-936F-472C-8F0F-095D57EB75B8_zpsaxtwvrhx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It wasn't all rainbows and unicorns though. It was hard because Archer didn't feel whole and he didn't think that he deserved Bree. <br><br>I am going to stop here because if I keep on I might give it away. <br><br>I will say that it was kind of long and I tend to get anxious when I read long books but it was totally worth it. <br><br>Some of my favorite quotes!!!<br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/25E0BCC1-4C20-48AA-BE36-DB61C704913C_zps4abpzira.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478745603i/21107607._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 25E0BCC1-4C20-48AA-BE36-DB61C704913C_zps4abpzira.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/D694EF7B-1859-4BA8-BFBD-F92E85957229_zps7g4m3zbv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478745603i/21107608._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo D694EF7B-1859-4BA8-BFBD-F92E85957229_zps7g4m3zbv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/80CC38C5-22FA-46BF-986B-CF3980789FC6_zpsxq0hcw9c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478745603i/21107609._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 80CC38C5-22FA-46BF-986B-CF3980789FC6_zpsxq0hcw9c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer9473624733565300340"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>I am definitely in the minority on this, but I just didn't <i>love </i> this one as much as most of my friends seemed to. <br/><br/>Don't get me wrong, it had a lot of really sweet elements and themes weaved throughout the story (e.g. the whole dandelion thing), and Archer and Bree were really cute (if somewhat flat?) characters, but it was just missing something for me. <br/><br/>Probably just me though.</span>

<div id="review_839162483" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/839162483" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/839162483?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=sugary-sweet">sugary-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=love">love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=heart-breaking-gut-wrenching">heart-breaking-gut-wrenching</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer839162483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10830101452671746569">4--<b>My Heart....My Emotions....Just Give Me a Moment</b>--Stars!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391200577ra/8347693.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'll just be....yeah<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388053704ra/7729627.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Archer, Archer, Archer I just want to give you the biggest freakin' hug. <br/><br/>I found <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20639274.Archer_s_Voice__Sign_of_Love___4_' title='Archer's Voice (Sign of Love, #4) by Mia Sheridan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Archer's Voice</a> to be very melancholy....just the overall theme. The story itself was beautiful and emotional and my heart broke and I cried. And I wanted so bad for Archer to find peace and happiness. <br/><br/>This was definitely a slower pace then I prefer....less dialogue than I prefer. But it was a really insipiring read and in the end I was h</span>
  <span id="freeText10830101452671746569" style="display:none">4--<b>My Heart....My Emotions....Just Give Me a Moment</b>--Stars!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391200577ra/8347693.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'll just be....yeah<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388053704ra/7729627.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Archer, Archer, Archer I just want to give you the biggest freakin' hug. <br><br>I found <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20639274.Archer_s_Voice__Sign_of_Love___4_" title="Archer's Voice (Sign of Love, #4) by Mia Sheridan" rel="nofollow noopener">Archer's Voice</a> to be very melancholy....just the overall theme. The story itself was beautiful and emotional and my heart broke and I cried. And I wanted so bad for Archer to find peace and happiness. <br><br>This was definitely a slower pace then I prefer....less dialogue than I prefer. But it was a really insipiring read and in the end I was happy. It was just a journey getting there.<br><br>Archer Hale witnessed a horrific tragedy at the age of seven that changed his life. In the blink of an eye he lost his parents and his uncle and he was left unable to speak. He lived a life of solitude and lonliness until he meets Bree.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391201652ra/8348033.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bree Prescott is running. Running from her own tragedy she escapes to Pelion, Maine. She's on her own little road trip of self-discovery. She rents a little cabin near the lake and gets a job at the local diner. And one day she meets Archer. <br><br>Archer and Bree become friends. For the first time Archer believes in having more. That maybe something good can come from the tragedy of his past. <br><br>Bree and Archer fall in love. And it's beautiful and it's heart breaking. Watching Archer navigate through life experiences that he knew nothing about. Learning to trust again and believe that love is possible, even for him. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Someday … when we're old and gray, I'm going to look at you lying in bed beside me, just like this, and I'm going to look into your eyes and know that it's only ever been you. And that is going to be the great joy of my life.” </i>
</b><br><br>I loved that there wasn't a lot of juvenile drama. It was Archer learning to live in a world that was so unfamiliar to him. Communicating with people for the first time. <br><br><b>
  <i>"His eyes told me everything… We communicated a thousand words, without a single one being spoken."</i>
</b><br><br>Exposing himself and opening himself up to heart break and possibility. Wanting more. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I knew I loved her – fiercely and with every part of my heart, even the broken parts, even the parts that felt unworthy and without value. And maybe those parts most of all.”</i>
</b><br><br>Travis:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391118055ra/8333579.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I do recommend this story, despite the slower pace and overall sad undertones. I have found all of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6994378.Mia_Sheridan" title="Mia Sheridan" rel="nofollow noopener">Mia Sheridan</a>'s books to be very different and I have liked them all in their own way. I fell in love with Archer the boy and Archer the man. Bree saved him. Bree was his home. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Only you, only ever you."</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10830101452671746569" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1957644807?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1957644807" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9119495921081482265"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 2/1/2014)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 4/3/2017)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This is definitely one of my all time favorite books! The H, Archer, is the best! I think it would've been easy to make his character into a beta male because of his life, but I LOVE how Ms. Sheridan made him have automatic alpha-male tendencies! It's not a huge secret that I'm not big on beta males even when I feel for their trauma, so this was kind-of a huge deal for me in making me love his character! I also love </span>
  <span id="freeText9119495921081482265" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 2/1/2014)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 4/3/2017)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This is definitely one of my all time favorite books! The H, Archer, is the best! I think it would've been easy to make his character into a beta male because of his life, but I LOVE how Ms. Sheridan made him have automatic alpha-male tendencies! It's not a huge secret that I'm not big on beta males even when I feel for their trauma, so this was kind-of a huge deal for me in making me love his character! I also love the stories where two damaged souls find peace and happiness in each other, and I think Ms. Sheridan is one of (if not <i>the</i>) best at creating these stories. If you've been living under a rock ;) and haven't checked out this book yet -- you need to meet you're new ultimate book boyfriend, Archer, ASAP!<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Bree and Archer's story. Bree is on the run from her past, and ends up in a small town in Maine. She learns about the town mystery man by bumping into him one day, and is instantly drawn to him. After some awkward encounters, they form a friendship of sorts that eventually turns into more. Both of them carry a lot of baggage from their traumatic pasts that they have to work through, they have some sexy times, and they fall in love...and get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Bree (mostly) and Archer's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they take a while to develop stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 5+ stars! I think he has to be one of my all time favorite Hs! He is so innocent, naive, and sweet -- BUT he also has an instinctive possessiveness and alpha-maleness (probably not a word)...so he becomes the best type of dichotomy to make the perfect bbf!<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Bree. I liked her. She was a super kind person at heart, and I love how she saw something in Asher and didn't give up.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>I didn't cry this go-round, but I remember crying the first time I read it.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H is majorly weary of strangers/other people at first and pushes the h away. The H also leaves for a time. They both pursue the relationship at times.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Hot. They have some hot tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mentions of birth control. I don't remember any mention of previous practices for the h, and the H was a virgin.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H's cousin pursues the h and causes some drama. The h also has a long-time male friend that shows up that causes a little bit of drama. The H gets tricked into going to a strip bar and ends up in a private room with a stripper that gives him a lap dance. He knew her from when he was younger and crushed on her. She makes him touch her breasts and I believe it is implied he orgasms. This is after feelings have developed between the h and H. While I didn't consider this cheating because I feel like he was tricked and it was a unique situation, I understand that some readers might consider it so. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for ~3 months, and there was mention that neither of them had other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Violence/murder/domestic violence/alcoholism/cheating (side characters - off page through memories), loss of parents (off page), H has damaged vocal cords and cannot talk, virgin H, and violence (on page).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> It had great closure with a jump ahead epilogue and a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I paid $3.99 for it on Amazon back in 2014.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a ~3 week separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_1802125722" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1802125722" />
    <a title="Mischenko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1194517-mischenko"><img alt="Mischenko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587209348p2/1194517.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1802125722?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mischenko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mischenko" href="/user/show/1194517-mischenko">Mischenko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32851571-archer-s-voice">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1802125722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1148868976085549526">This book is featured on Throwback Thursday @ <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://readrantrockandroll.com/2018/01/18/throwback-thursday-archers-voice-by-mia-sheridan-january-18th/#more-31703'>https://readrantrockandroll.com/2018/...</a><br/><br/>I found <i>Archer’s Voice</i> floating around on Goodreads sometime in 2016 and went right to Amazon to grab a copy. The story grabbed my attention from the very first words.<br/><br/>Bree has moved to a little town in Maine. She’s looking for a new start and finds herself a little cabin to move into. After finding a job at a diner and meeting some new people in town, she runs into a man named Archer. Archer looks fairly dishev</span>
  <span id="freeText1148868976085549526" style="display:none">This book is featured on Throwback Thursday @ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readrantrockandroll.com/2018/01/18/throwback-thursday-archers-voice-by-mia-sheridan-january-18th/#more-31703">https://readrantrockandroll.com/2018/...</a><br /><br />I found <i>Archer’s Voice</i> floating around on Goodreads sometime in 2016 and went right to Amazon to grab a copy. The story grabbed my attention from the very first words.<br /><br />Bree has moved to a little town in Maine. She’s looking for a new start and finds herself a little cabin to move into. After finding a job at a diner and meeting some new people in town, she runs into a man named Archer. Archer looks fairly disheveled and at first she can’t figure out what it is, but she sees something in him. Why on Earth won’t he talk to her? She’s persistent and reaches out to Archer in hope for a breakthrough, but Arthur has been damaged. He’s been shown unkindness far too many times and Bree has her work cut out for her. The angst is almost unbearable.<br /><br /><i>“I’m afraid to love you. I’m afraid that you’ll leave and that I’ll go back to being alone again. Only it will be a hundred times worse because I’ll know what I’m missing. I can’t…” He sucked in a shaky breath. “I want to be able to love you more than I fear losing you, and I don’t know how. Teach me, Bree. Please teach me. Don’t let me destroy this.”</i> —<b>Archer</b><br /><br />I just loved Bree and Archer’s characters. Bree is so kind-hearted and she’s willing to go the extra mile to break through to Archer and help him heal. She’s battling her own demons and both of them need to overcome the pain they’ve experienced in the past. Archer is equally kind, but he needs help materializing everything–someone patient, caring, and willing to give him a chance. He has to learn to trust again.<br /><br />This was a favorite in 2016 and I hope more people who enjoy reading romance will pick this one up. It’s wonderful. I’m thinking this will be a reread in 2018 for me. I rated this one 5*****.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1148868976085549526" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1094768597" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1094768597" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1094768597?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=turtles-are-slow">turtles-are-slow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=cheese-puffs">cheese-puffs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1094768597" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3674949536658027306"><b>4 stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414977445i/11713038._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I honestly wasn’t planning on reading this book just yet but my crazy fingers swiped on it, the book opened, hours flew by, and whaddya know? I’m through with the book. As for my rating, it took me some time to decide as I was spinning between the 3 and 5 star range. I mean, I liked the book. I loved it actually. But I didn’t <b>
  <u>LOVE</u>
</b> it. The praise for this book is absolutely warranted though. The deep emotional pull and one of the very best literary heroes is probably enough to give t</span>
  <span id="freeText3674949536658027306" style="display:none"><b>4 stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414977445i/11713038._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I honestly wasn’t planning on reading this book just yet but my crazy fingers swiped on it, the book opened, hours flew by, and whaddya know? I’m through with the book. As for my rating, it took me some time to decide as I was spinning between the 3 and 5 star range. I mean, I liked the book. I loved it actually. But I didn’t <b>
  <u>LOVE</u>
</b> it. The praise for this book is absolutely warranted though. The deep emotional pull and one of the very best literary heroes is probably enough to give this book 5 stars, but as much as I am a romantic at heart I have very cynical tastes and there were too many coincidences in the story along with a few particular scenes I wasn’t fond of and so that made me think 3 stars. But no matter what parts of the book I loved or disliked, at the heart of everything is this beautiful man Archer who I loved like crazy and I can’t bring myself to 3 star him…so 4 stars it is to account for both the parts I enjoyed and struggled with. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414977445i/11713039._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The heroine Bree Prescott has been through a traumatic ordeal and in an effort to escape those lingering memories, ditches her home and arrives at a small town in Maine hoping for some peace. Bree is a very likable heroine who is both lovely and kind, and for someone who is afflicted with terrors and understandable trust issues, she easily makes new friends, gets a new job, catches the eye of the town’s most eligible bachelor, and is the first to coax out the reclusive hero Archer Hale in just days. And while her goal in town is simply to try to live without fear and looking over her shoulder, she can’t help but feel a connection to Archer and a desire to want to know him more.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414977445i/11713040._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Archer Hale. Honestly one of the best heroes I’ve <i>ever</i> read, Archer has suffered through a childhood experience no kid should have to go through. He’s misunderstood by the townspeople as an eccentric loner because no one will take the chance to get to know the real him. No one but Bree. <br><br>I think it’s easy to mix up sympathy for love and while some of my love for this character does stem from sympathy, most is from an admiration of how much Archer suffered through, both physical and emotional agony, to get to where he is today, and his efforts in making his relationship with Bree work despite his social stigma. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414977445i/11713041._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As much as I loved everything about Archer, some things in this story bothered me, like Bree just happening to be the only one who could communicate with him with sign language. And the whole ‘one person politically and financially controls the town’ theme. Then there was a specific Travis/Archer scene that really pissed me off and then the ending scene, no matter how appropriate it might be, came off as cheesy and overly sweet as if <i>all</i> the loose ends had to be tied up in a nice, neat bow. And then when Bree’s past caught up with her, that secondary plotline felt underdeveloped and haphazardly thrown together. I get that this story’s main focus is the romance and that’s perfectly OK, but by doing so the author really does ignore the minor plotlines running parallel to the romance. <br><br>This is a book that has very strong and compelling main characters but because the book focus is solely on the romance, the actual storyline is inherently weak. Nevertheless, the writing is beautiful, evocative and triggers deep emotions and the hero was extraordinary, so I think this book is worth reading for those reasons alone. <br><br><u>Archer’s Voice</u> is the 4th book in the Sign of Love series and a complete standalone. It is not related to any of the books in this series and is a story inspired by Sagittarius.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3674949536658027306" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_810662477" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/810662477" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/810662477?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2014-release">2014-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer810662477" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10785049326438402957"><br/>★★★★★ <b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“...the loudest words are the ones we live.”</i>
</blockquote> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400687476i/9707993.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This story was absolutely <b>BEAUTIFUL</b>.<br/><br/>Ever since I first read Stinger and later on Leo and Leo's Chance, Mia Sheridan has become one of my favorite contemporary romance authors. She just has a way of storytelling that completely resonates with me and that makes me fall in love with the characters and their epic love story each and every time. And Archer's voice was no exception. Once again, this was a wonderful story that made laugh an</span>
  <span id="freeText10785049326438402957" style="display:none"><br>★★★★★ <b>5 Stars!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“...the loudest words are the ones we live.”</i>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400687476i/9707993.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story was absolutely <b>BEAUTIFUL</b>.<br><br>Ever since I first read Stinger and later on Leo and Leo's Chance, Mia Sheridan has become one of my favorite contemporary romance authors. She just has a way of storytelling that completely resonates with me and that makes me fall in love with the characters and their epic love story each and every time. And Archer's voice was no exception. Once again, this was a wonderful story that made laugh and cry and swoon all at once. It's a story that will forever hold a special place in my heart and that I would highly recommend <i>everyone</i> to give a try, whether you're a romance fan or not.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Sometimes an understanding silence was better than a bunch of meaningless words.” </i>
</blockquote><br>✦ <b>Bree Prescott</b> ✦<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400694773i/9708973.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Bree arrives in the sleepy, lakeside town of Pelion, Maine, all she wants is to find peace. Peace from the nightmares and memories that still haunt her six months after the event that uprooted her life. That event made her weary and heartbroken, but she's determined to start over and she hopes a new environment is the key to a fresh start. Her strength and ability to see the best in people made Bree a very likable and easy to relate to heroine and I loved her quirky side and sense of humor.<br><br>✦ <b>Archer Hale</b> ✦<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400694773i/9708974.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>An accident as a child has made Archer Hale lose his voice. The events that unfolded after said accident and his inability to speak have caused him to live a life in solitude - a life where loneliness has become the norm. As a hero, he's sweet, shy, caring and fiercely protective all at once. *MAJOR SWOON* It takes a while for him to open himself up to Bree and the friendship she's offering but once he finds out that she truly wants to get to know him and spend time with him, he comes completely out of his shell. Together, Bree and Archer find ways to communicate and heal each other, beyond all barriers his inability might present. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"His eyes told me everything… We communicated a thousand words, without a single one being spoken."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400689267i/9708354.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Archer's disability to express himself out loud provides many challenges in his relationship not only with Bree, but with everyone around him. He's spent many years by himself, without any form of communication with anyone other than his uncle and he has a lot to learn when it comes to relationships and intimacy, but he's a fast learner and Bree is patient and willing enough to help him become the best version of himself possible. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I want to be able to love you more than I fear losing you, and I don't know how. Teach me, Bree. Please teach me. Don't let me destroy this.” </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Bree and Archer's relationship is one that slowly but surely evolves from deep friendship to all-consuming love but that has quite a few bumps along the road. Miscommunication, circumstances and people that want to keep them apart...but overall there wasn't a huge amount of angst in the story, just the right amount to keep the story from ever becoming boring or predictable. Most chapters are from Bree's POV but I loved the fact that we also get a chapter from Archer's POV every now and then; they made me understand his history and reasonings much better.<br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>"I think love is a concept, and each person has an individual word for what sums it up for them. My word for love is Bree.” </i>
</blockquote><br>All in all, Archer's Voice was an unputdownable, unforgettable story about love, hope, loss, friendship and healing that will from now on reside on my all-time-favorites-shelf. <br><br><b>Standalone.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400687476i/9707995.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
<i>“I was finally home. Not the place, but his arms. Archer’s arms were my home- the only place I wanted to be, the place where I felt safe. The place where I felt loved.”</i> </blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="10785049326438402957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1768850200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10088622689605595953"><b>4.5 EMOTIONALLY HEARD STARS</b><br/><br/>So I finally read a book by Mia Sheridan, and I must say <b> I LOVED IT!</b><br/><br/>This book is about two emotional scared individuals who come together to form a couple.<br/>They both have to overcome their demons that haunt their dreams nightly. <br/>Archer was such a sympathetic character to me at first. I could understand why the heroine Bree was captivated by him. I loved when Bree makes mention of his working outside would make a commercial success as a workout with the result being you</span>
  <span id="freeText10088622689605595953" style="display:none"><b>4.5 EMOTIONALLY HEARD STARS</b><br><br>So I finally read a book by Mia Sheridan, and I must say <b> I LOVED IT!</b><br><br>This book is about two emotional scared individuals who come together to form a couple.<br>They both have to overcome their demons that haunt their dreams nightly. <br>Archer was such a sympathetic character to me at first. I could understand why the heroine Bree was captivated by him. I loved when Bree makes mention of his working outside would make a commercial success as a workout with the result being you would look like Archer. <br><b>CAUSE THAT MAN WAS FINE.</b><br>However, the things he signs to Bree at the beginning are very disturbing:<br><i>"..Sometimes I feel like everything is over my head. It makes me feel...weak and angry, and not worthy of you. Not worthy of anything. ( you are so worthy here Archer)<br>"If you had not come back I would have lay here until I died. I would have just willed myself to die."<br>"I'm not even a man. I can't fight for you." </i><br>I think it's safe to say he suffers from low self-esteem here and with abandonment issues.<br>Archer is connected with Bree and even without his voice, Archer could be heard by Bree.<br>She is able to use sign language communicate with him and it's almost Kismet that they meet each other here. They are a great couple and have had to over come so much to be together. Their struggle felt REAL and their emotions were so RAW. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474980028ra/20664922.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However, I could not give it the full 5 stars as the hero left the heroine to "find himself." This was not a bad thing here but he left her without even writing her a word and he could have written her a letter letting her know he was okay and not dead. But NOOOO he chooses to be an ass and left her to worry about him and he does not EVEN GROVEL here. He left her to face her first Christmas alone after the murder of her father, knowing it would be hard for her. He told her how he was with this random family.....I WAS SO F*CKING MAD, I WANTED TO SMACK HIS FACE OFF. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474980191ra/20664942.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bree was a complete SAINT here taking him back after all the shit worry he put her through. She may be the most accepting person in fiction I have ever read about. She helps him overcome his speech limitations, she understood when he would not communicate with her when he was he went to that strip club, what he did, why he did it, she even forgave him abandoning her ON CHRISTMAS and his birthday. Really she is the best and at the end, she was way way too good for him.<br><i>"You ran from me, and I died a little more each day! You didn't even let me know that you were safe! Why?" Again, Bree you are such a Saint.</i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474979918i/20664911.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I loved this ugly cry inducing book that made me feel like a was a part of their story. Like I was not an observer but an active participant. That is why I will read more books from this author. <br>Despite the content here, I was able to see past all that and allow myself to feel the words. That quality of writing is very rare and when I find an author that can move me like this, I read their books. <br><b>I may not always like the content of the book, but the quality of the writing is Superb</b><br>Worth a read and a reread for me <i>later here much later</i><br><br>Also, this book has an awesome epilogue that has us seeing them 5 years later. LOVE AN EPILOGUE LIKE THAT. <br><br>Safety: this book is safe with exception <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[hero goes to strip club and gets a hard on by another and allows her to touch him <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, little to no OW/OM drama (a male friend of hers come to visit her that had a crush on her little drama from that). She has experience with 3 past lovers and he is a virgin.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10088622689605595953" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1262979642" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1262979642" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1262979642?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1262979642" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8225829527304710357"><b>5 **<u>I lost my heart to you.</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458300768i/18468182.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Someday … when we're old and gray, I'm going to look at you lying in bed beside me, just like this, and I'm going to look into your eyes and know that it's only ever been you. And that is going to be the great joy of my life.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Thank you to my blogging partner in crime Sandy. She has been bugging me for ages to discover <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6994378.Mia_Sheridan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mia Sheridan's</a> books and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice' rel='nofollow noopener'>Archer's Voice</a> in particular. And what a success it has been. Hit me right in the feels. Beautifully writte</span>
  <span id="freeText8225829527304710357" style="display:none"><b>5 **<u>I lost my heart to you.</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458300768i/18468182.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Someday … when we're old and gray, I'm going to look at you lying in bed beside me, just like this, and I'm going to look into your eyes and know that it's only ever been you. And that is going to be the great joy of my life.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Thank you to my blogging partner in crime Sandy. She has been bugging me for ages to discover <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6994378.Mia_Sheridan" rel="nofollow noopener">Mia Sheridan's</a> books and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice" rel="nofollow noopener">Archer's Voice</a> in particular. And what a success it has been. Hit me right in the feels. Beautifully written, wonderful characters and an incredibly moving love story. Really a special little gem.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I didn’t know enough to dream you, Bree, but somehow you came true anyway. How did that happen?” He rubbed his nose along mine, pausing and then pulling back again. “Who read my mind and knew exactly what I wanted, even when I didn’t?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Bree Prescott</b> is looking for peace and a way to deal with a very traumatic experience and she finds herself in a small town in Maine. A fateful place for her and just like magic a lot of things suddenly fall into place. A sweet rental house, a lovely next door neighbour who helps her find a job and most importantly <b>Archer Hale</b>. The man without a voice and lots of secrets, she quite literally runs into. They have an instant connection and since Bree has a hard time staying away from him - a beautiful friendship develops. <br><br>Both characters need each other in some way or another. Archer has lead a very isolated life, hiding himself from the world and Bree functions as a catalyst to pull him out of his shell, giving him hope. In return Archer is the safety and peace Bree so desperately needs. And together they create magic. Very corny way of putting it, but it is kind of true. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I think love is a concept, and each person has an individual word for what sums it up for them. My word for love is Bree.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The best part about this book? ARCHER HALE!<br><br>Oh my god. What a character. So vulnerable and strong all at the same time. He is damaged by his past both physically and emotionally. But still he is the most honest, caring and resilient person I have ever met in written form. Simply beautiful. All the surrounding characters are very well written and Bree is his perfect counterpart, but Archer absolutely makes this book what it is. <br><br>Bottom line...GO READ!! This book is worth a try. It showcases all I've grown to love about Ms. Sheridan's books. A feel good read, a carefully constructed and slowly paced romance with a lot of heart, emotion and the occasional heartbreak. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447539995i/17017465.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

<div id="review_3357759878" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3357759878" />
    <a title="Lianne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/108025953-lianne"><img alt="Lianne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601222731p2/108025953.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3357759878?book_show_action=true">May 30, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lianne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lianne" href="/user/show/108025953-lianne">Lianne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20639274-archer-s-voice">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/108025953-lianne?shelf=2020-faves">2020-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/108025953-lianne?shelf=all-time-faves">all-time-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/108025953-lianne?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3357759878" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17781508896861900110"><b>𝟱 "𝗜 𝗰𝗮𝗺𝗲 𝗵𝗲𝗿𝗲 𝗳𝗼𝗿 𝘆𝗼𝘂" 𝘀𝘁𝗮𝗿𝘀✨</b><br/><br/>Don't mind me. this is just me thinking about this book.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590853657ra/29567109.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is one of those books that will stay on my mind for a very very long time. I'm in complete awe. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>"his eyes told me everything that his voice couldn't. We communicated a thousand words, without a single one being spoken."</b>
</i><br/><br/>The pacing is just perfect. Not too fast and not too slow either. I'm never bored while reading this. I wish I'm as understanding and as strong as Bree and Archer. Our awkward boy sweet,</span>
  <span id="freeText17781508896861900110" style="display:none"><b>𝟱 "𝗜 𝗰𝗮𝗺𝗲 𝗵𝗲𝗿𝗲 𝗳𝗼𝗿 𝘆𝗼𝘂" 𝘀𝘁𝗮𝗿𝘀✨</b><br><br>Don't mind me. this is just me thinking about this book.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590853657ra/29567109.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is one of those books that will stay on my mind for a very very long time. I'm in complete awe. <br><br><i>
  <b>"his eyes told me everything that his voice couldn't. We communicated a thousand words, without a single one being spoken."</b>
</i><br><br>The pacing is just perfect. Not too fast and not too slow either. I'm never bored while reading this. I wish I'm as understanding and as strong as Bree and Archer. Our awkward boy sweet, silent Archer Hale. They are the softest. Protect them at all cost. ♡♡♡♡<br><br><i>
  <b>"I didn't know enough to dream you, Bree, but somehow you came true anyway. How did that happen? He rubbed his nose along mine, pausing and then pulling back again. Who read my mind and knew exactly what I wanted, even when I didn't?"</b>
</i><br><br>Btw that specific scene at the end..I almost had a heart attack. I nearly threw my phone away. My poor heart is literally pounding so loud lmao. This was surprisingly moving for me maybe due to the fact that I don't know anything about this book. I just randomly said 'alright you've been sitting on my TBR for so long let's try you now'. Thank freak I read this. I clearly have no idea what I've been missing.<br><br>"𝓛𝓸𝓿𝓮 𝔀𝓪𝓼 𝓪𝓵𝓵 𝓪𝓫𝓸𝓾𝓽 𝓵𝓮𝓪𝓻𝓷𝓲𝓷𝓰 𝓽𝓸 𝓼𝓹𝓮𝓪𝓴 𝓪 𝓹𝓮𝓻𝓼𝓸𝓷'𝓼 𝓵𝓪𝓷𝓰𝓾𝓪𝓰𝓮."</span>
  <a data-text-id="17781508896861900110" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('lKBzfkBYJFcuDLLCJiEntsJxD7vtv6hJcBvJq1iSQpWuhhqs+wbtP4knBqPR1C1pFC7ocyMyJi4rZY8aldGwDw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3fVparsNmijxAwoh7veQ3C7huSEcdr7hJ7lKkVPTP6Hn0wC4AFNTQFYovkAZApoD+L5e6dL7MIZ8xwwgnpDNOw==')})
  }
